                        pages: i,
                        pageParams: s

                      , b = C(r, E);
                    l = await h(E, b, g)
                } else {

                        if (a > 0 && C == null)
                            break;
                        l = await h(l, C),
                        a++
                    } while (a < g)
                }
                return l
            }
            ;
            t.options.persister ? t.fetchFn = ()=>{
                var d, S;
                return (S = (d = t.options).persister) == null ? void 0 : S.call(d, u, {
                    queryKey: t.queryKey,
                    meta: t.options.meta,
                    signal: t.signal
                }, n)
            }

        }
    }
}

function ag(e) {

function WS(e, t, n) {

function df(e, t) {

function QS(e, t, n) {

    n === void 0 && (n = !0),

      , o = "^" + e.replace(/\/*\*?$/, "").replace(/^\/*/, "/").replace(/[\\.*+^${}|()[\]]/g, "\\$&").replace(/\/:([\w-]+)(\?)?/g, (s,l,a)=>(r.push({

function KS(e) {

        return e.split("/").map(t=>decodeURIComponent(t).replace(/\//g, "%2F")).join("/")
    } catch (t) {

        e
    }
}
function ug(e, t) {

        return e;
    if (!e.toLowerCase().startsWith(t.toLowerCase()))

      , r = e.charAt(n);
    return r && r !== "/" ? null : e.slice(n) || "/"
}
